<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропеллер.html>пропе́ллер</a> (22798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропеллер.html>пропе́ллер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propéller</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропеллер.html>пропе́ллера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропеллер.html>пропе́ллеры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропеллер.html>пропе́ллеров</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропеть.html>пропе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sing</li>
<li>to sing <i>(for some time)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пропеть.html>пропе́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>у́тро</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní <b>propéli</b> vsjó útro.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They <b>sang</b> throughout the morning.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропивать.html>пропива́ть</a> (23938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропить.html>пропи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропивать.html>пропива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропить.html>пропи́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прописать.html>прописа́вший</a> (7555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прописать.html>прописа́ть</a> (7555)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописать.html>прописа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописывать.html>пропи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prescribe <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">medicine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<li>to record <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">information</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***прописка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прописка.html>пропи́ска</a> (8085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописать.html>прописа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propisátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to register</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописка.html>пропи́ска</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propíska</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописка.html>пропи́ски</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописка.html>пропи́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописка.html>пропи́сок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>propiska, residence permit, (mandatory) registration (<i>USSR</i>)</li>
<li>the stamp in the Soviet <i>internal passport</i> (serving as a personal ID) with the registered address.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>, place where one lives (as stated in the stamp)</li></ol>

***прописной.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прописной.html>прописно́й</a> (22901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропись.html>про́пись</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">própisʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописной.html>прописно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propisnój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>conventional, trivial, commonplace, common
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прописной.html>прописна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мораль.html>мора́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>propisnája</b> morálʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">conventional morality; copy-book morality; copy-book maxims</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прописной.html>прописна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:истина.html>и́стина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>propisnája</b> ístina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(boring) truism; copy-book truth, common truth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>upper-case, capital (letter)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прописной.html>прописна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́ква</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>propisnája</b> búkva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">capital letter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cursive (letter)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:прописной.html>прописны́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:буква.html>бу́квы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>propisnýje</b> búkvy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cursive (script)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пропись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропись.html>про́пись</a> (28482)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прописать.html>прописа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропись.html>про́пись</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">própisʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропись.html>про́писи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропись.html>про́писи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропись.html>про́писей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prescription</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cursive sample sheet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cliche, platitude</li>
<li>handwriting among printed text</li>
<li>font imitating handwriting, such as true italics</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">painting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> preliminary drawing on canvas, used to guide the finished painting</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропитать.html>пропита́ть</a> (9076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропитать.html>пропита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:питать.html>пита́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропитаться.html>пропита́ться</a> (22853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропитать.html>пропита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропитаться.html>пропита́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propitátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пропи́тываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be imbued, to be saturated, to be soaked</li>
<li>to be impregnated</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропитать.html>пропита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропитывать.html>пропи́тывать</a> (27794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропитать.html>пропита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропитывать.html>пропи́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propítyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропитать.html>пропита́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to impregnate <i>(with)</i>, to saturate <i>(with)</i>, to soak <i>(in)</i>, to steep <i>(in)</i></li></ol>

***пропить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропить.html>пропи́ть</a> (17343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропить.html>пропи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропивать.html>пропива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend/squander on drink
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пропить.html>пропи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вещь.html>ве́щи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>propítʹ</b> véšči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sell one's things to get money for drink; swap one's things for drink</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ruin through drinking
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пропить.html>пропи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>propítʹ</b> gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ruin/lose one's voice through drinking</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***проплывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проплывать.html>проплыва́ть</a> (11215)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проплыть.html>проплы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proplýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проплывать.html>проплыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proplyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проплыть.html>проплы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swim by, to float by, to sail by
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1998</b>,  Александр Суханов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Sukhanov" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Sukhanov">Alexander Sukhanov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:дракон.html>Драко́н</a></cite>  | <cite>Dragon Playing the Violin</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>Там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принцесса.html>принце́сса</a> кита́я <a href = vnd.unilang:однажды.html>одна́жды</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проплывать.html>проплыва́я</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ла</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>Так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыграть.html>сыгра́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:финал.html>фина́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дивный.html>ди́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сыграть.html>сыгра́л</a>...</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tam princéssa Kitája odnáždy, <b>proplyvája</b>, skazála: ne káždyj Tak sygrál by finál, kak on dívno sygrál...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Once, a Chinese princess, sailing by, said: not everyone would play the finale the amazing way he did...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to swim (a certain distance or time), to sail (a certain distance or time)</li></ol>

***проплыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проплыть.html>проплы́ть</a> (14205)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плыть.html>плыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проплыть.html>проплы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proplýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проплывать.html>проплыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swim by, to float by, to sail by</li>
<li>to swim (a certain distance or time), to sail (a certain distance or time)</li></ol>

***проповедовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проповедовать.html>пропове́довать</a> (12057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пропове́дать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propovédatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проповедовать.html>пропове́довать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">propovédovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пропове́дать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">church</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to preach, to sermonize</li>
<li>to propagate, to advocate</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пропове́дать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">propovédatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проповедь.html>про́поведь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">própovedʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проповедь.html>про́поведи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проповедь.html>про́поведи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проповедь.html>про́поведей</a></b>)
